   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Legal drinking age</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Alkoholersterwerbsalter_(Weltweit)2.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Alkoholersterwerbsalter_%28Weltweit%292.svg/500px-Alkoholersterwerbsalter_%28Weltweit%292.svg.png" decoding="async" width="500" height="254" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Alkoholersterwerbsalter_%28Weltweit%292.svg/750px-Alkoholersterwerbsalter_%28Weltweit%292.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Alkoholersterwerbsalter_%28Weltweit%292.svg/1000px-Alkoholersterwerbsalter_%28Weltweit%292.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1410" data-file-height="715"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Alkoholersterwerbsalter_(Weltweit)2.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Minimum legal age to purchase alcohol by country (2015):</b>
         <br>
         <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r981673959">.mw-parser-output .legend{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .legend-color{display:inline-block;min-width:1.25em;height:1.25em;line-height:1.25;margin:1px 0;text-align:center;border:1px solid black;background-color:transparent;color:black}.mw-parser-output .legend-text{}</style>
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#000000; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Prohibited regardless of age
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#441200; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age is 25
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#7F0000; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age is 21
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#FF0000; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age is 20
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#B200FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age is 19
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0026FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age is 18
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#00FFFF; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age is 17
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#267F00; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age is 16
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#00FF00; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age is 15
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#B9B9B9; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;No regulation/no age set
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The <b>legal drinking age</b> is the minimum age at which a person can <a href="/wiki/Legally" class="mw-redirect" title="Legally">legally</a> consume <a href="/wiki/Alcoholic_beverage" class="mw-redirect" title="Alcoholic beverage">alcoholic beverages</a>. The minimum age alcohol can be legally consumed can be different from the age when it can be purchased in some countries. These laws vary between countries and many laws have exemptions or special circumstances. Most laws apply only to <a href="/wiki/Drinking_in_public" title="Drinking in public">drinking alcohol in public places</a> with alcohol consumption in the home being mostly unregulated (an exception being the UK, which has a minimum legal age of five for supervised consumption in private places). Some countries also have different age limits for different <a href="/wiki/List_of_alcoholic_drinks" title="List of alcoholic drinks">types of alcohol drinks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-IARD_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IARD-1">[1]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>The most commonly known reason for the law behind the legal drinking age is the <a href="/wiki/Long-term_impact_of_alcohol_on_the_brain" title="Long-term impact of alcohol on the brain">effect on the brain</a> in adolescents. Since the brain is still maturing, alcohol can have a <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_alcohol_on_memory" title="Effects of alcohol on memory">negative effect on the memory</a> and long-term thinking. Alongside that, it can cause <a href="/wiki/Alcoholic_liver_disease" title="Alcoholic liver disease">liver failure</a>, and create a <a href="/wiki/Long-term_effects_of_alcohol_consumption#Hormonal_imbalance" class="mw-redirect" title="Long-term effects of alcohol consumption">hormone imbalance</a> in teens due to the constant changes and maturing of hormones during <a href="/wiki/Puberty" title="Puberty">puberty</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> Young people are also especially at increased risk of injury when drinking alcohol.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> They may not have the necessary knowledge of low-risk drinking. Indeed, public health researchers found that people’s age at drinking the first full serve of alcohol was significantly associated with knowledge of low-risk drinking and drinks counting. The levels of knowledge of low-risk drinking and frequency of drinks counting increased with age at first drink of alcohol more steeply during adolescence than in the later period.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Africa">Africa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_drinking_age&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Africa">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Drinking_age_Africa.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Drinking_age_Africa.svg/230px-Drinking_age_Africa.svg.png" decoding="async" width="230" height="230" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Drinking_age_Africa.svg/345px-Drinking_age_Africa.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Drinking_age_Africa.svg/460px-Drinking_age_Africa.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="1000"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Drinking_age_Africa.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Minimum legal age to purchase alcohol by country (2015):</b>
         <br>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#000000; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Prohibited
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#7F0000; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 21 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0026FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 18 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#00FFDD; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 17 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#267F00; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 16 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#00FF00; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 15 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#808080; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;No minimum purchase age
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The most common minimum age to purchase alcohol in Africa is 18. However, Angola (except Luanda Province), Central African Republic, Comoros, Equatorial Guinea, Guinea-Bissau, Mali, and Togo have no laws on the book restricting the sale of alcohol to minors. In Libya, Somalia and Sudan the sale, production and consumption of alcohol is completely prohibited.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research#Synthesis_of_published_material" title="Wikipedia:No original research"><span title="The material near this tag may be based upon an improper synthesis of sources. (October 2018)">improper synthesis?</span></a></i>]</sup> </p>

         <td>There is no national legislation prohibiting the sale of alcohol to minors. </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/Luanda_Province" title="Luanda Province">Luanda Province</a> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;" colspan="2">18<sup id="cite_ref-Decreto_Executivo_nº_87/08_de_10_julho_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Decreto_Executivo_nº_87/08_de_10_julho-8">[8]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Legislation in <a href="/wiki/Luanda_Province" title="Luanda Province">Luanda Province</a>: <p>It is prohibited to sell alcohol beverages to anyone under the age of 18. It is also prohibited for minors to buy and consume alcohol.<sup id="cite_ref-Decreto_Executivo_nº_87/08_de_10_julho_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Decreto_Executivo_nº_87/08_de_10_julho-8">[8]</a></sup> </p> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Flag_of_Benin.svg/23px-Flag_of_Benin.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Flag_of_Benin.svg/35px-Flag_of_Benin.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Flag_of_Benin.svg/45px-Flag_of_Benin.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Benin" title="Benin">Benin</a> </td> 
         <td align="center">None </td> 
         <td align="center">20 </td> 
         <td>Republic of Benin Report to UN Committee on the Rights of the Child CRC/C/BEN/2 (2005): 
          <ul>
           <li>Article 8 of the decree of 10 June 1942 regulating the production, import, advertisement, sale, and consumption of alcohol beverages in French West Africa, prohibits the sale or free supply of alcohol beverages to minors under 20.</li> 
           <li>Article 13 stipulates fines ranging from CFAF 200,000 to CFAF 1 million for such offences, doubled in the case of repeat offences.</li> 
           <li>There are no official measures prohibiting children from consuming alcohol, tobacco or other substances harmful to their health.</li>
          </ul> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_Botswana.svg/23px-Flag_of_Botswana.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_Botswana.svg/35px-Flag_of_Botswana.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_Botswana.svg/45px-Flag_of_Botswana.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Botswana" title="Botswana">Botswana</a> </td> 
         <td align="center">None<sup id="cite_ref-Botswana_Liquor_Act_2008_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Botswana_Liquor_Act_2008-9">[9]</a></sup> <small>(prohibited for any person to supply)</small><sup id="cite_ref-ACPF:_MINIMUM_AGE_FOR_SALE_OF_ALCOHOL_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ACPF:_MINIMUM_AGE_FOR_SALE_OF_ALCOHOL-7">[7]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-Botswana_Liquor_Act_2008_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Botswana_Liquor_Act_2008-9">[9]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited for any person with a liquor license to sell or supply alcohol beverages to minors under the age of 18 years. Because the law only applies to licensees, it is not prohibited for minors to buy, consume, or possess alcohol beverages.<sup id="cite_ref-Botswana_Liquor_Act_2008_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Botswana_Liquor_Act_2008-9">[9]</a></sup> It is also prohibited for any person to expose or supply alcohol to a minor under the age of 18 years.<sup id="cite_ref-ACPF:_MINIMUM_AGE_FOR_SALE_OF_ALCOHOL_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ACPF:_MINIMUM_AGE_FOR_SALE_OF_ALCOHOL-7">[7]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Flag_of_Burundi.svg/23px-Flag_of_Burundi.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Flag_of_Burundi.svg/35px-Flag_of_Burundi.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Flag_of_Burundi.svg/46px-Flag_of_Burundi.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Burundi" title="Burundi">Burundi</a> </td> 
         <td align="center">None<sup id="cite_ref-Code_Penal_Burundi_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Code_Penal_Burundi-10">[10]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td align="center">18 <small>(unless accompanied by parent or legal guardian)</small><sup id="cite_ref-Code_Penal_Burundi_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Code_Penal_Burundi-10">[10]</a></sup> </td>

        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Flag_of_Cameroon.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cameroon.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Flag_of_Cameroon.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cameroon.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Flag_of_Cameroon.svg/45px-Flag_of_Cameroon.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Cameroon" title="Cameroon">Cameroon</a> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">21 <small>(18 if accompanied by a person 21 years of age or older)</small><sup id="cite_ref-Cameroon_Penal_Code_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cameroon_Penal_Code-11">[11]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited for any person with a liquor license to sell or supply alcohol beverages to anyone under 18 years of age. The law permits adults from the ages 18 to 21 to consume, purchase and buy alcohol beverages if accompanied by a person 21 years of age or older. Anyone over the age of 21 years may buy or consume alcohol unaccompanied. </td>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Flag_of_the_Central_African_Republic.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Central_African_Republic.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Flag_of_the_Central_African_Republic.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Central_African_Republic.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Flag_of_the_Central_African_Republic.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Central_African_Republic.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Central_African_Republic" title="Central African Republic">Central African Republic</a> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">15 <small>(off-premises)</small>, or 21 <small>(on-premises)</small><sup id="cite_ref-:1_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-13">[13]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited for any person to sell or supply alcohol beverages to minors under the age of 15 years when sold or supplied off-premises (e.g., liquor stores, wine stores, and supermarkets). It is prohibited for any person to sell or supply alcohol beverages to minors under the age of 21 years when sold or supplied on-premises (e.g., restaurants, bars, and cafes).<sup id="cite_ref-:1_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-13">[13]</a></sup> </td>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Flag_of_Ethiopia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Ethiopia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Flag_of_Ethiopia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Ethiopia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Flag_of_Ethiopia.svg/46px-Flag_of_Ethiopia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> </td> 
         <td align="center">15<sup id="cite_ref-Penal_of_Ethiopia_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Penal_of_Ethiopia-17">[17]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-Penal_of_Ethiopia_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Penal_of_Ethiopia-17">[17]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited for any person to sell, offer, serve or allow to serve alcohol beverages "in substantial quantities" to any infant or young person. The criminal code defines a young person as any person under the age of 15 years. But the Criminal Code Proclamation 414 (2004) states: "Whoever endangers the health of another, intentionally and unscrupulously, by administering or serving, or by causing or permitting to be administered or served, to minors (defined as anyone under the age of 18 years) (...) alcohol beverages or spirituous liquors of such kind or in such quantity as to make their injurious effect certain or probable, is punishable with simple imprisonment not exceeding one year, and fine. <p>The Revised Family Code Proclamation No. 213 (2000) Article 215 defines a minor as anyone who has not attained the full age of 18. </p> </td>
        </tr>

(b) sell or deliver liquor, cigarettes or tobacco products to, or allow liquor to be consumed or cigarettes or any tobacco products to be used by any person under the age of 18 years on the premises; ... (i) admit any person under the age of 18 years to a premises licensed as a public bar, toddy bar or at the premises licensed to manufacture and sell baka or lapire;...</li>

         <td align="center">18 (except with parent/guardian consent)<br> </td> 
         <td>Liquor Act Article 116 Prohibited conduct by persons in general (1) No person shall— ... (l) being a person to whom in terms of this Act the sale of liquor is prohibited, purchase or attempt to purchase liquor in contravention of such provision; .... (o) sell, lend, give, supply or deliver, or offer so to do, any liquor to any person under the age of eighteen years except with the consent of the parent or guardian of that person. <p>Children's Act Section 78 - It is prohibited for any person to sell, lend, give, supply, deliver or offer alcohol beverages to any child under the age of 16 years, except upon production of a written order signed by the parent or guardian of the child known to such person. The police has the duty to seize any alcohol beverage in the possession of a child under the age of 16 years without a written consent of the parents or legal guardian.<sup id="cite_ref-CHILDREN’S_ACT_ZIMBABWE_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CHILDREN’S_ACT_ZIMBABWE-36">[36]</a></sup> </p> </td>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Americas">Americas</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_drinking_age&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Americas">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Drinking_age_North_America.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Drinking_age_North_America.svg/230px-Drinking_age_North_America.svg.png" decoding="async" width="230" height="277" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Drinking_age_North_America.svg/345px-Drinking_age_North_America.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Drinking_age_North_America.svg/460px-Drinking_age_North_America.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1789" data-file-height="2154"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Drinking_age_North_America.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Minimum legal age to purchase alcohol by country:</b>
         <br>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#7F0000; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 21 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#B200FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 19 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0026FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 18 years
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Alkoholersterwerbsalter_in_Zentralamerika_und_der_Karibik.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Alkoholersterwerbsalter_in_Zentralamerika_und_der_Karibik.png/230px-Alkoholersterwerbsalter_in_Zentralamerika_und_der_Karibik.png" decoding="async" width="230" height="176" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Alkoholersterwerbsalter_in_Zentralamerika_und_der_Karibik.png/345px-Alkoholersterwerbsalter_in_Zentralamerika_und_der_Karibik.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Alkoholersterwerbsalter_in_Zentralamerika_und_der_Karibik.png/460px-Alkoholersterwerbsalter_in_Zentralamerika_und_der_Karibik.png 2x" data-file-width="670" data-file-height="513"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Alkoholersterwerbsalter_in_Zentralamerika_und_der_Karibik.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Minimum legal age to purchase alcohol by country:</b>
         <br>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0026FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 18 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#267F00; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 16 years
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Drinking_age_South_America.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Drinking_age_South_America.svg/230px-Drinking_age_South_America.svg.png" decoding="async" width="230" height="308" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Drinking_age_South_America.svg/345px-Drinking_age_South_America.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Drinking_age_South_America.svg/460px-Drinking_age_South_America.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="454" data-file-height="608"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Drinking_age_South_America.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Minimum legal age to purchase alcohol by country (2015):</b>
         <br>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#FF0000; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 20 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0026FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 18 years
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/Central_America" title="Central America">Central America</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">Caribbean</a>, and <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South America</a> the legal drinking age and legal purchase age varies from 0 to 20 years (see table below). In <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South America</a> in particular, the legal purchase age is 18 years, with two exceptions: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>In <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a>, the legal drinking age and purchase age is 20 years.</li> 
       <li>In <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">Guyana</a>, minors aged 16 or 17 may consume a glass of beer or wine in a restaurant provided they buy a meal.</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a> the legal drinking age and legal purchase age varies from 18 to 21 years: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>In <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>, it is 18 for each.</li> 
       <li>In the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, the minimum legal age to purchase any alcohol beverage from a shop, supermarket, liquor store, bar, club or any other licensed premises is 21 years of age; the two exceptions are <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Virgin_Islands" title="United States Virgin Islands">Virgin Islands</a> where the age is 18. The legal drinking age varies by state.</li> 
       <li>In <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, most provinces have a minimum age of 19 years to buy or consume alcohol, while <a href="/wiki/Alberta" title="Alberta">Alberta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Manitoba" title="Manitoba">Manitoba</a> and <a href="/wiki/Quebec" title="Quebec">Quebec</a> set it at 18 years.</li>
      </ul>
      <p> In the late 20th century, much of North America changed its minimum legal drinking ages (MLDAs) as follows: <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r996844942">.mw-parser-output .templatequote{overflow:hidden;margin:1em 0;padding:0 40px}.mw-parser-output .templatequote .templatequotecite{line-height:1.5em;text-align:left;padding-left:1.6em;margin-top:0}</style></p>
      <blockquote class="templatequote">
       <p>In the 1970s, provincial and state policy makers in Canada and the United States moved to lower MLDAs (which were set at 21 years in most provinces/territories and states) to coincide with the jurisdictional <a href="/wiki/Age_of_majority" title="Age of majority">age of majority</a> — typically 18 years of age.... As a result, MLDAs were reduced in all Canadian provinces [and] in <a href="/wiki/U.S._history_of_alcohol_minimum_purchase_age_by_state" title="U.S. history of alcohol minimum purchase age by state">more than half of US states</a>. In Canada, however, two provinces, Ontario [in 1979] and Saskatchewan [in 1976], quickly raised their subsequent MLDAs from 18 to 19 years in response to a few studies demonstrating an association between the lowered drinking age and increases in alcohol-related harms to youth and young adults, including increases in <a href="/wiki/Motor_vehicle_accidents" class="mw-redirect" title="Motor vehicle accidents">motor vehicle accidents</a> (MVAs) and <a href="/wiki/Alcohol_intoxication" title="Alcohol intoxication">alcohol intoxication</a> among high school students. Following MLDA reductions in the US, research in several states provided persuasive evidence of sharp increases in rates of fatal and nonfatal MVAs appearing immediately after the implementation of lower drinking ages. These scientific findings galvanized public pressure on lawmakers to raise MLDAs and, in response, the federal government introduced the <a href="/wiki/National_Minimum_Drinking_Age_Act" title="National Minimum Drinking Age Act">National Minimum Drinking Age Act</a> of 1984, which imposed a reduction of highway funds for states if they did not increase their MLDA to 21 years. All states complied and implemented an MLDA of 21 years by 1988.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup></p>
      </blockquote>

         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18<sup id="cite_ref-Alberta_GAMING_AND_LIQUOR_ACT_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Alberta_GAMING_AND_LIQUOR_ACT-46">[46]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Manitoba_The_Liquor_and_Gaming_Control_Act_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Manitoba_The_Liquor_and_Gaming_Control_Act-47">[47]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Quebec_ACT_RESPECTING_LIQUOR_PERMITS_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Quebec_ACT_RESPECTING_LIQUOR_PERMITS-48">[48]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>In Alberta no person may give or sell or permit any person to give or sell liquor to a minor in licensed premises.<sup id="cite_ref-Alberta_GAMING_AND_LIQUOR_ACT_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Alberta_GAMING_AND_LIQUOR_ACT-46">[46]</a></sup> In Manitoba a person must not give, sell or otherwise supply liquor to a minor. The law provides exceptions for a doctor, dentist, pharmacist or other health care professional for medical purposes; for sacramental purposes and by the parent, guardian, spouse or common-law partner, if it is given or supplied in a residence.<sup id="cite_ref-Manitoba_The_Liquor_and_Gaming_Control_Act_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Manitoba_The_Liquor_and_Gaming_Control_Act-47">[47]</a></sup> In Quebec the law prohibits the sale of alcohol beverages to a minor under the age of 18 years.<sup id="cite_ref-Quebec_ACT_RESPECTING_LIQUOR_PERMITS_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Quebec_ACT_RESPECTING_LIQUOR_PERMITS-48">[48]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">19 </td> 
         <td>Ontario's <a href="/wiki/Liquor_Licence_Act_(Ontario)" title="Liquor Licence Act (Ontario)">Liquor Licence Act</a> permits the supply and consumption of liquor to those under the age of 19. However, supplying a person under the age of 19 is restricted to the person's parent or legal guardian, and may only occur in a residence or in a private place of the parent or legal guardian. A person under the age of 19 who was supplied liquor in this manner is permitted to consume the liquor only in the place it was supplied.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup> </td>

         <td colspan="2"><i><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">Cayman Islands</a></i> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18<sup id="cite_ref-LIQUOR_LICENSING_LAW_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LIQUOR_LICENSING_LAW-50">[50]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited to sell, serve or supply alcohol beverages to anyone under the age of 18 years. It is also prohibited for any minor to buy, attempt to buy or consume alcohol beverages. Violation of the law is punished with a fine of five thousand dollars, and the court may, if the offence was committed by the licensee, order that the licensee shall forfeit his licence and that no licence may be issued to that person for a period not exceeding ten years from the date of his conviction. </td>

         <td>The minimum age is 18 to enter an enclosure that sells alcohol beverages. Selling alcohol to a minor may incur a fine. One must provide identification upon request. Residents of Chile over the age of 18 must carry their <a href="/wiki/Identity_card#Chile" class="mw-redirect" title="Identity card">Chilean identification card</a> issued by the Civil Registry and Identification Service at all times.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup> </td>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Flag_of_Costa_Rica.svg/23px-Flag_of_Costa_Rica.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Flag_of_Costa_Rica.svg/35px-Flag_of_Costa_Rica.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Flag_of_Costa_Rica.svg/46px-Flag_of_Costa_Rica.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica" title="Costa Rica">Costa Rica</a> </td>

         <td>The law prohibits the sale of alcohol to a minor (anyone under the age of 18 years). Selling alcohol to a minor will be punished with a fine equivalent to ten basic salaries. Whoever permits minors to maintain in any establishment which main purpose is to sell alcohol beverages, will be sanctioned with a fine equivalent to five salaries. It is not prohibited for minors to buy, attempt to buy or consume alcohol.<sup id="cite_ref-Costa_Rica_Ley_n.º_7633_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Costa_Rica_Ley_n.º_7633-53">[53]</a></sup> </td>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Flag_of_Cuba.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cuba.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Flag_of_Cuba.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cuba.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Flag_of_Cuba.svg/46px-Flag_of_Cuba.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a> </td>

         <td align="center">16<sup id="cite_ref-Cuba_CODIGO_PENAL_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuba_CODIGO_PENAL-54">[54]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>The penal code prohibits any adult to induce any young person under the age of 16 years, to habitually consume alcohol beverages. However this means that de facto anyone selling, serving or supplying alcohol should check if the buyer has attained the age of 16 years. In most cases this law is not strictly enforced.<sup id="cite_ref-Cuba_CODIGO_PENAL_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cuba_CODIGO_PENAL-54">[54]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup> </td>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Flag_of_Ecuador.svg/23px-Flag_of_Ecuador.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Flag_of_Ecuador.svg/35px-Flag_of_Ecuador.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Flag_of_Ecuador.svg/45px-Flag_of_Ecuador.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1440" data-file-height="960">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a> </td>

         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-Ley_Ecuador_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ley_Ecuador-57">[57]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited to sell alcohol beverages to a minor under the age of 18 years of age. The law obligates establishments to place a visible notice at the point of sale and to check identification to enforce the law. However it is not prohibited for minors to buy, attempt to buy or consume alcohol.<sup id="cite_ref-Ley_Ecuador_57-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ley_Ecuador-57">[57]</a></sup> </td>

        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg/23px-Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="13" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg/35px-Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg/46px-Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1005" data-file-height="567">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/El_Salvador" title="El Salvador">El Salvador</a> </td> 
         <td align="center">None </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-LEY_REGULADORA_DE_LA_PRODUCCION_Y_COMERCIALIZACION_DEL_ALCOHOL_Y_DE_LAS_BEBIDAS_ALCOHOLICAS_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEY_REGULADORA_DE_LA_PRODUCCION_Y_COMERCIALIZACION_DEL_ALCOHOL_Y_DE_LAS_BEBIDAS_ALCOHOLICAS-58">[58]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is strictly prohibited to sell or serve alcohol beverages to a minor under the age of 18 years. Violation of the law is punished with ¢ 25,000.00 and if convicted once more the license will be suspended for a period of six months. It is legal for minors to buy, attempt to buy and consume alcohol.<sup id="cite_ref-LEY_REGULADORA_DE_LA_PRODUCCION_Y_COMERCIALIZACION_DEL_ALCOHOL_Y_DE_LAS_BEBIDAS_ALCOHOLICAS_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEY_REGULADORA_DE_LA_PRODUCCION_Y_COMERCIALIZACION_DEL_ALCOHOL_Y_DE_LAS_BEBIDAS_ALCOHOLICAS-58">[58]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><i><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/83/Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Falkland_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a></i> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18<sup id="cite_ref-Control_of_Drinking_by_Juveniles_Ordinance_1993_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Control_of_Drinking_by_Juveniles_Ordinance_1993-59">[59]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited for any adult to sell, give or provide alcohol to a minor under the age of 18 years in any public place or licensed premises. Parents may permit their children to consume alcohol on private premises. Minors consuming alcohol in public are committing a criminal offence. The law provides exceptions for the consumption of alcohol by minors for prescription of or at the direction of a government medical officer or in the course of the administration of Holy Communion according to the rites of any Christian denomination.<sup id="cite_ref-Control_of_Drinking_by_Juveniles_Ordinance_1993_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Control_of_Drinking_by_Juveniles_Ordinance_1993-59">[59]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

The law has not yet been approved and enacted. <p><i>Law prohibiting minors entry to entertainment venues</i> Article 1 prohibits those under the age of 16 from entering cinemas and theaters (except during children's programming), clubs, cafes, or venues licensed to sell alcohol beverages. </p> </td>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1235" data-file-height="650">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a><br>(50 states) </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;">Varies by state<sup id="cite_ref-IARD_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IARD-1">[1]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;">21<sup id="cite_ref-IARD_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IARD-1">[1]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>The <a href="/wiki/National_Minimum_Drinking_Age_Act" title="National Minimum Drinking Age Act">National Minimum Drinking Age Act</a> (established in 1984) requires all states and territorites to have a minimum purchasing age of 21 in order to be eligible for federal highway funding, though the age of consumption is left at the state-level. Only two U.S. territorites have a drinking age of 18, those being Puerto Rico and the U.S. Virgin Islands. <p>Some <a href="/wiki/U._S._state" class="mw-redirect" title="U. S. state">states</a> do not allow those under the legal drinking age to be present in liquor stores or in <a href="/wiki/Bar_(establishment)" class="mw-redirect" title="Bar (establishment)">bars</a> (usually, the difference between a bar and a <a href="/wiki/Restaurant" title="Restaurant">restaurant</a> is that food is served only in the latter). Contrary to popular belief, only a few states prohibit <a href="/wiki/Minor_(law)" title="Minor (law)">minors</a> and <a href="/wiki/Youth" title="Youth">young adults</a> from consuming alcohol in private settings. </p><p>The National Institute on Alcohol Abuse and Alcoholism maintains a database that details state-level regulations on consumption and sale age limits.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup> </p> 
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Minor_in_Possession" title="Minor in Possession">Minor in Possession</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_alcohol_laws_of_the_United_States" title="List of alcohol laws of the United States">List of alcohol laws of the United States</a>
          </div> </td>
        </tr>

         <td>Food Act 1983 Food Regulations (1985) Regulation 361 (2014) and Food (Amendment) Regulations 2016 <p>Increased from 18 to 21 in December 2017, effective October 16, 2018. There will be an 18-month grace period for sellers to comply. After the grace period, anyone caught selling to persons under 21 can be fined up to RM10,000 and jailed up to 2 years.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup> </p><p><a href="/wiki/Malaysian_identity_card" title="Malaysian identity card">Malaysian identity cards</a> include a designation of religion, which allows enforcement of the religion-based sales restriction. </p> </td>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Singapore.svg/23px-Flag_of_Singapore.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Singapore.svg/35px-Flag_of_Singapore.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Singapore.svg/45px-Flag_of_Singapore.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="4320" data-file-height="2880">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a> </td>

         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-:3_98-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-98">[98]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited to sell alcohol to those under 18. Anyone caught selling, furnishing or acquiring alcohol in any licensed premise to persons below 18 can be fined up to $10,000. <p>It is also prohibited for minors to purchase, or attempt to purchase alcohol from any licensed premises, in which the minors can also be fined up to $10,000. However, the authorities rarely enforced this on minors. </p><p>It is technically legal for minors to possess and consume alcohol at home and in public (not in any licensed premises) as there is no law prohibiting it. It is also technically legal for someone to purchase alcohol and pass it to minors outside the store or licensed premise.<sup id="cite_ref-:3_98-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-98">[98]</a></sup> </p> </td>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/45px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> </td> 
         <td align="center">None </td> 
         <td align="center">19<sup id="cite_ref-law.go.kr_99-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-law.go.kr-99">[99]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>The age limit for alcohol is 19 calculated by the year of birth. This means that an 18-year-old will be legally allowed to purchase and consume alcohol if he or she will be turning 19 that year. For example, two persons born on January 1st, 2002 and December 31st, 2002 will both turn 19 years of age at the same time on January 1st, 2021 and hence, both of them will be considered to be of legal age to purchase and consume alcohol on and after that date, despite the latter being only 18 years and 1 day old based on western age. <p>The method of calculating the legal age for alcohol slightly differs from Korean age reckoning in which another one year will be added to the person's age, whereas this method only doesn't take into account the month and day of birth but only the year instead. <sup id="cite_ref-law.go.kr_99-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-law.go.kr-99">[99]</a></sup> </p> </td>
        </tr>

         <td align="center">21<br>Completely prohibited in Sharjah </td> 
         <td>In November 2020, Drinking became legal in UAE without requiring a license and regardless of the religion.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup> <p>Previously, expatriate non-<a href="/wiki/Muslim" class="mw-redirect" title="Muslim">Muslim</a> residents had to request a liquor permit to purchase alcohol beverages, but it was prohibited for such holders to provide drinks to others.<sup id="cite_ref-Guidelines_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guidelines-108">[108]</a></sup> </p><p>The legal age for drinking alcohol is 18 in Abu Dhabi (although a Ministry of Tourism by-law allows hotels to serve alcohol only to those over 21), and 21 in Dubai and the Northern Emirates (except Sharjah, where drinking alcohol is prohibited).<sup id="cite_ref-:0_106-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-106">[106]</a></sup> </p><p>It is a punishable offence to drink, or to be under the influence of alcohol, in public.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_106-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-106">[106]</a></sup> </p> </td>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Flag_of_Uzbekistan.svg/23px-Flag_of_Uzbekistan.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Flag_of_Uzbekistan.svg/35px-Flag_of_Uzbekistan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Flag_of_Uzbekistan.svg/46px-Flag_of_Uzbekistan.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan" title="Uzbekistan">Uzbekistan</a> </td> 
         <td align="center">None </td> 
         <td align="center">20 <sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Vietnam.svg/23px-Flag_of_Vietnam.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Vietnam.svg/35px-Flag_of_Vietnam.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Vietnam.svg/45px-Flag_of_Vietnam.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> </td> 
         <td align="center">18 </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-IARD_1-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IARD-1">[1]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Decree 94/2012/ND-CP on Liquor Production and Trading (2012), Article 19.7 </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Flag_of_Yemen.svg/23px-Flag_of_Yemen.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Flag_of_Yemen.svg/35px-Flag_of_Yemen.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Flag_of_Yemen.svg/45px-Flag_of_Yemen.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;" colspan="2">Prohibited<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Exception is in <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a> Region where it's legal for 21 and up<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Europe">Europe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_drinking_age&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Europe">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Drinking_age_Europe.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Drinking_age_Europe.svg/500px-Drinking_age_Europe.svg.png" decoding="async" width="500" height="382" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Drinking_age_Europe.svg/750px-Drinking_age_Europe.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Drinking_age_Europe.svg/1000px-Drinking_age_Europe.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="680" data-file-height="520"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Drinking_age_Europe.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Minimum legal age to purchase alcohol by country (2015):</b>
         <br>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#FF0000; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 20 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0026FF; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 18 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#00FFDD; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 17 years
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#267F00; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum purchase age of 16 years
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Konsumverbot.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Konsumverbot.svg/500px-Konsumverbot.svg.png" decoding="async" width="500" height="382" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Konsumverbot.svg/750px-Konsumverbot.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Konsumverbot.svg/1000px-Konsumverbot.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="680" data-file-height="520"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Konsumverbot.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Laws banning minors from consuming alcohol in public/private:</b>
         <br>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#FF0000; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age to consume alcohol in public and private
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#FFD800; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Minimum age to consume alcohol in public
         </div>
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#267F00; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;No minimum age to consume alcohol in public or private
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>Most countries in <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> have set 18 as the minimum age to purchase alcohol. Although <a href="/wiki/Austria" title="Austria">Austria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Liechtenstein" title="Liechtenstein">Liechtenstein</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg" title="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> (except <a href="/wiki/Ticino" class="mw-redirect" title="Ticino">Ticino</a>) maintain a minimum purchase age below 18 years permitting minors either full or limited access to alcohol. In 2005,<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup> 2007<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup> and 2015<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup> harmonization at the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> level toward a minimum purchase age of 18 was discussed, but not agreed. </p>
      <p>Timeline of changes to drinking/purchase age or laws restricting the access to alcohol for minors: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>In 2002 the Spanish autonomous communities <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">Madrid</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Valencia" title="Valencia">Valencia</a><sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">Catalonia</a><sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup> raised their minimum purchase age to 18 years. Previously, Valencia and Madrid had a minimum purchase age of 16 years, and in Catalonia minors aged 16 or 17 could purchase alcohol up to 23% ABV on- and off-premise.</li> 
       <li>In 2004 <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a><sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">[118]</a></sup> raised its off-premise purchase age from 15 to 16 years.</li> 
       <li>In November 2005 Switzerland passed its Food and Commodities Regulation<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">[119]</a></sup> (German: Lebensmittel- und Gebrauchsgegenständeverordnung), introducing a ban on alcohol sales to anyone under the age of 16. The Alcohol Law<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">[120]</a></sup> (German: Alkoholgesetz) passed in 1980 requires a minimum age of 18 years for the retail sale of distilled spirits. Therefore, it is prohibited to sell fermented alcohol (e.g. <a href="/wiki/Beer" title="Beer">beer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wine" title="Wine">wine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sparkling_wine" title="Sparkling wine">sparkling wine</a> or <a href="/wiki/Cider" title="Cider">cider</a>) to anyone under the age of 16, and any distilled alcohol beverages to anyone under the age of 18 years. The canton of Ticino has a cantonal law since 1989 that makes the purchase age limit for all alcohol beverages 18 years.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>In 2006 the Spanish autonomous community <a href="/wiki/Castile_and_Le%C3%B3n" title="Castile and León">Castile and León</a><sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup> raised its minimum purchase age from 16 to 18 years.</li> 
       <li>In late 2006, <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a><sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup> lawmakers passed the <i>Children and Young Persons (Alcohol, Tobacco and Gaming) Act 2006</i>, which raised the minimum purchase age from 16 to 18 years. But the new law made an exception: minors aged 16 or 17 can purchase and consume beer, wine or cider under 15% ABV on-premise, and pre-packed containers of an alcohol strength not exceeding 5.5% ABV (e.g. <a href="/wiki/Alcopops" class="mw-redirect" title="Alcopops">alcopops</a>).</li> 
       <li>In 2009 <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a><sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">[124]</a></sup> raised its minimum purchase age to 18 years,<sup id="cite_ref-SantePublique3_125-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SantePublique3-125">[125]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SantePublique4_126-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SantePublique4-126">[126]</a></sup> and fines were increased for selling or serving alcohol to a minor (up to €7,500). Previously, the minimum age was 16 years for off-premise and on-premise purchases of low-alcohol beverages (up to 3% ABV) such as wine, beer, cider, perry, mead, crème de cassis and juices from fermented fruits or vegetables that contain 1.2 to 3° alcohol, natural sweet wines from controlled cultivation and 18 for higher-ABV beverges.</li> 
       <li>In October 2009, the government of <a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup> passed a new law raising its drinking and purchase age from 16 to 17 years.</li> 
       <li>In 2010 the Spanish autonomous community of <a href="/wiki/Galicia_(Spain)" title="Galicia (Spain)">Galicia</a> raised its minimum purchase age from 16 to 18 years.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>In 2011 <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a><sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup> passed a law raising the minimum age for off-premise sale of alcohol beverages of &gt;16.5% ABV to 18 years of age. The minimum age to purchase alcohol beverages of &lt;16.5% ABV remains 16.</li> 
       <li>In March 2012 <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a> raised the minimum purchase age to 18, from 16 previously.<sup id="cite_ref-Art._30_130-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Art._30-130">[130]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LEGE_Nr._1100_131-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEGE_Nr._1100-131">[131]</a></sup></li> 
       <li><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> raised its minimum purchase age from 16 to 18 in 2012. Previously Italy did not have a purchase age for off-premise sales, and the minimum age of 16 years for on-premise sales was not well enforced.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>In 2013 the government of <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a> restricted alcohol sales to young people: distilled spirits cannot be sold to anyone under the age of 18, and other alcohol beverages (e.g. beer, wine, or cider) cannot be sold to anyone under the age of 16. Previously the minimum age for all alcohol beverages was 16 years.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>As of 1&nbsp;January&nbsp;2014<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legal_drinking_age&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, the minimum legal purchase and consumption age was raised from 16 to 18 in the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a>. Previously young people over the age of 16 could purchase and consume alcohol beverages of &lt;15% ABV, and those aged 18 and over could purchase all alcohol beverages.<sup id="cite_ref-Alcohol_in_de_wet_134-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Alcohol_in_de_wet-134">[134]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>As of March&nbsp;2015<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legal_drinking_age&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, the Spanish autonomous community of <a href="/wiki/Asturias" title="Asturias">Asturias</a> raised its drinking age from 16 to 18 years. Asturias was Spain's last community with a drinking age of 16 years. The new law brings the drinking age into line with the rest of Spain, with the exception of Baleares Islands where no purchase age limit is set.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>As of December&nbsp;2015<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legal_drinking_age&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a> harmonized its minimum drinking age to 18 years across all beverage types. Previously the purchase age was 16 years for low-alcohol beverages such as beer, wine or cider.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>As of 1&nbsp;January&nbsp;2018<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legal_drinking_age&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, <a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a> raised its minimum drinking age from 18 to 20 years.<sup id="cite_ref-Seimas_adopted_amendments_on_reduction_of_alcohol_consumption_137-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Seimas_adopted_amendments_on_reduction_of_alcohol_consumption-137">[137]</a></sup></li> 
       <li>From January 2019 the federal states of <a href="/wiki/Austria" title="Austria">Austria</a> decided to align their drinking and purchase ages. The states <a href="/wiki/Burgenland" title="Burgenland">Burgenland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lower_Austria" title="Lower Austria">Lower Austria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vienna" title="Vienna">Vienna</a> therefore raised their age limits for alcohol beverages containing spirits to 18. Prior to 2019 these states had a general drinking and purchase age of 16 years. The sale and consumption of beer, wine and other fermented alcohol beverages is now prohibited to children and young people under the age of 16 years, and the sale and consumption of spirits to minors under the age of 18 years is prohibited throughout Austria.<sup id="cite_ref-austria_138-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-austria-138">[138]</a></sup></li>
      </ul>

        </tr>

         <th colspan="2" style="width:20%;">Purchase age </th>

         <th style="width:5%;">Private </th> 
         <th style="width:5%;">Public </th>

         <th style="width:5%;">Off-premise </th>

        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Flag_of_Albania.svg/21px-Flag_of_Albania.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Flag_of_Albania.svg/32px-Flag_of_Albania.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Flag_of_Albania.svg/42px-Flag_of_Albania.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="980" data-file-height="700">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-albania_140-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-albania-140">[140]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-albania_140-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-albania-140">[140]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>The sale of alcohol beverage in bars, restaurants or other licensed premises, as well as other points of sale, is prohibited to minors under the age of 18 years. Vendors and operators of licensed premises are required to post a clearly legible notice in A4 format stating "Ndalohet shitja e alkoolit personave nën 18 vjeç" (It is prohibited to sell alcohol beverages to people under 18 years). Consumption by those under age 18 in public places is prohibited.<sup id="cite_ref-albania_140-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-albania-140">[140]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Andorra.svg/22px-Flag_of_Andorra.svg.png" decoding="async" width="22" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Andorra.svg/33px-Flag_of_Andorra.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Andorra.svg/43px-Flag_of_Andorra.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="700">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Andorra" title="Andorra">Andorra</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None<sup id="cite_ref-andorra_141-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-andorra-141">[141]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;">18<sup id="cite_ref-andorra_141-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-andorra-141">[141]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18<sup id="cite_ref-andorra_141-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-andorra-141">[141]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Selling, serving or supplying alcohol beverages is prohibited as well as public consumption of alcohol beverage by minors under the age of 18 years.<sup id="cite_ref-andorra_141-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-andorra-141">[141]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Flag_of_Armenia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Armenia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Flag_of_Armenia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Armenia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Flag_of_Armenia.svg/46px-Flag_of_Armenia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None<sup id="cite_ref-ՎԱՐՉԱԿԱՆ_ԻՐԱՎԱԽԱԽՏՈՒՄՆԵՐԻ_ՎԵՐԱԲԵՐՅԱԼ_ՀԱՅԱՍՏԱՆԻ_ՀԱՆՐԱՊԵՏՈՒԹՅԱՆ_ՕՐԵՆՍԳԻՐՔ_142-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ՎԱՐՉԱԿԱՆ_ԻՐԱՎԱԽԱԽՏՈՒՄՆԵՐԻ_ՎԵՐԱԲԵՐՅԱԼ_ՀԱՅԱՍՏԱՆԻ_ՀԱՆՐԱՊԵՏՈՒԹՅԱՆ_ՕՐԵՆՍԳԻՐՔ-142">[142]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-ՎԱՐՉԱԿԱՆ_ԻՐԱՎԱԽԱԽՏՈՒՄՆԵՐԻ_ՎԵՐԱԲԵՐՅԱԼ_ՀԱՅԱՍՏԱՆԻ_ՀԱՆՐԱՊԵՏՈՒԹՅԱՆ_ՕՐԵՆՍԳԻՐՔ_142-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ՎԱՐՉԱԿԱՆ_ԻՐԱՎԱԽԱԽՏՈՒՄՆԵՐԻ_ՎԵՐԱԲԵՐՅԱԼ_ՀԱՅԱՍՏԱՆԻ_ՀԱՆՐԱՊԵՏՈՒԹՅԱՆ_ՕՐԵՆՍԳԻՐՔ-142">[142]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>There are no laws mandating alcohol vendors to ID potential underage drinkers. ID checks are very rarely, if ever, carried out<sup id="cite_ref-ՎԱՐՉԱԿԱՆ_ԻՐԱՎԱԽԱԽՏՈՒՄՆԵՐԻ_ՎԵՐԱԲԵՐՅԱԼ_ՀԱՅԱՍՏԱՆԻ_ՀԱՆՐԱՊԵՏՈՒԹՅԱՆ_ՕՐԵՆՍԳԻՐՔ_142-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ՎԱՐՉԱԿԱՆ_ԻՐԱՎԱԽԱԽՏՈՒՄՆԵՐԻ_ՎԵՐԱԲԵՐՅԱԼ_ՀԱՅԱՍՏԱՆԻ_ՀԱՆՐԱՊԵՏՈՒԹՅԱՆ_ՕՐԵՆՍԳԻՐՔ-142">[142]</a></sup> Criminal Code the Republic of Armenia (2003), Article 166: "Involvement, by a person who reached 18 years, of a child into regular use of alcohol drinks... is punished with correctional labor for up to 1 year, or with arrest for the term of 1-2 months, or with imprisonment for the term of 5 years" </td>
        </tr>

         <td>The age limits are set out by the legislation of each federal state but where harmonized in January 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-austria_138-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-austria-138">[138]</a></sup> Carinthia also requires16-18-year-olds to maintain a blood alcohol level below 0.05%.<sup id="cite_ref-Rauchen_und_Alkohol_143-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rauchen_und_Alkohol-143">[143]</a></sup> </td>

         <td colspan="2" style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None<sup id="cite_ref-Vente_et_consommation_d’alcool_en_Belgique_146-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vente_et_consommation_d’alcool_en_Belgique-146">[146]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">18 for distilled beverages of higher than 1.2%ABV and fermented beverages of higher than 22%ABV <p>16 for other alcohol beverages<sup id="cite_ref-Vente_et_consommation_d’alcool_en_Belgique_146-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vente_et_consommation_d’alcool_en_Belgique-146">[146]</a></sup> </p> </td> 
         <td>Since 10 January 2010, it is prohibited to "sell, serve, or offer" any distilled alcohol beverages to those under the age of 18 or any alcohol beverage to those under 16.<sup id="cite_ref-Vente_et_consommation_d’alcool_en_Belgique_146-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vente_et_consommation_d’alcool_en_Belgique-146">[146]</a></sup> Previously, it was prohibited to sell alcohol drinks to under-16s, but accompanying adults could buy drinks for them. </td>

         <td colspan="2" style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None<sup id="cite_ref-Drinking_age_Bosnia_147-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Drinking_age_Bosnia-147">[147]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-Drinking_age_Bosnia_147-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Drinking_age_Bosnia-147">[147]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Selling alcohol to a minor under the age of 18 years is an offence. The law does not prohibit minors from buying, attempting to buy or consuming alcohol.<sup id="cite_ref-Drinking_age_Bosnia_147-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Drinking_age_Bosnia-147">[147]</a></sup> 
          <ul>
           <li>Law on Public Peace and Order (2015) Article 25 prohibits providing alcohol beverages to minors.</li> 
           <li>Law on Internal Trade (2010), Article 10 prohibits the sale in the retail trade of alcohol beverages to persons under 18 years of age.</li>
          </ul> </td>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/20px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/31px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/40px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="387">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None<sup id="cite_ref-dansk_153-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dansk-153">[153]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-dansk_153-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dansk-153">[153]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td align="center">16 <sup>(beverages of &lt;16.5% <a href="/wiki/ABV" class="mw-redirect" title="ABV">ABV</a>)</sup> <br> 18 <sup>(beverages of ≥16.5% <a href="/wiki/ABV" class="mw-redirect" title="ABV">ABV</a>)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-dansk_153-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dansk-153">[153]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>While there is no age requirement for drinking alcohol beverages in Denmark, there are laws that prohibit minors from buying alcohol from on-premise and off-premise outlets. <p>If a shop or bar fails to ask for an ID card and is identified having sold alcohol to an underage, it is subject to fine. A national ID card, obtained in the local town hall, can serve as age verification.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> This card is rarely used though since a passport or driver's license is more commonly used.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup> </p><p>Both the legal drinking and purchasing age in the Faroe Islands is 18.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup> </p> </td>
        </tr>

         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_Estonia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Estonia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_Estonia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Estonia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Flag_of_Estonia.svg/46px-Flag_of_Estonia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="990" data-file-height="630">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a> </td>

         <td>It is prohibited to sell, serve or supply alcohol beverages to anyone under the age of 18 years. Alcohol found in possession of any child can be confiscated by the police. </td>
