        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Finland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Finland.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Finland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Finland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Finland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Finland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1800" data-file-height="1100">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Finland" title="Finland">Finland</a> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18 <sup>(1.2–22% ABV)</sup><br>20 <sup>(&gt;22% ABV)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-alkoholilaki_158-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-alkoholilaki-158">[158]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;">18 <sup id="cite_ref-alkoholilaki_158-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-alkoholilaki-158">[158]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td style="text-align:center;">18 <sup>(1.2–22% ABV)</sup><br>20 <sup>(&gt;22% ABV)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-alkoholilaki_158-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-alkoholilaki-158">[158]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>All major grocery chains have implemented a policy to ask for ID if the customer looks under 30.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup> Stores may refuse to sell alcohol if the customer is accompanied by a minor, or if proxy purchasing is suspected. Purchasing alcohol on behalf of a minor is a criminal offence.<sup id="cite_ref-alkoholilaki_158-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-alkoholilaki-158">[158]</a></sup> <p>Police may search minors in public places and confiscate or destroy any alcohol beverages in their possession. Incidents are reported to the legal guardian and social authorities, who may intervene with child welfare procedures. In addition, those aged 15 or above are subject to a fine.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup> </p><p>In private, offering alcohol to a minor is considered a criminal offence if it results in drunkenness and the act can be deemed reprehensible as a whole, considering the minor's age, degree of maturity and other circumstances.<sup id="cite_ref-alkoholilaki_158-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-alkoholilaki-158">[158]</a></sup> </p> </td>
        </tr>

         <td colspan="2" align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-SantePublique2_161-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SantePublique2-161">[161]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> has no explicitly stated consumption age, but selling alcohol beverages to a minor (under 18) is prohibited and can be fined 7500 <a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">euros</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SantePublique2_161-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SantePublique2-161">[161]</a></sup> </td>

         <td colspan="2" style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None<sup id="cite_ref-Georgia_162-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Georgia-162">[162]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-Georgia_162-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Georgia-162">[162]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Under the Law on Protecting Minors from Harmful Influences 2001 the sale of alcohol beverages to minors is prohibited.<sup id="cite_ref-Georgia_162-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Georgia-162">[162]</a></sup> Juvenile Justice Code (2015) Article 3 defines minors as those under 18. </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None </td> 
         <td align="center">14<sup>(beer, wine and cider if accompanied)</sup><br>16 <sup>(beer, wine and cider)</sup><br>18 <sup>(spirits and foods containing spirits above negligible amounts)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-Germany_163-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Germany-163">[163]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">14<sup>(beer, wine and cider if accompanied)</sup><br>16 <sup>(beer, wine and cider)</sup><br>18 <sup>(spirits and foods containing spirits above negligible amounts)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-Germany_163-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Germany-163">[163]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited to sell, serve or supply fermented alcohol beverages (beer, wine, cider and sparkling wine) to anyone under 16 years of age. However this age limit drops down to 14 if a minor is accompanied by his parent or legal guardian. It is generally prohibited to serve, sell or supply any beverage containing spirits and foods containing spirits above negligible amounts, to anyone under the age of 18 years. Violation of the "Protection of Young Persons Act" can be fined up to €50,000.<br>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Alcohol_laws_in_Germany" title="Alcohol laws in Germany">Alcohol laws in Germany</a>
          </div>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Protection_of_Young_Persons_Act_(Germany)" title="Protection of Young Persons Act (Germany)">Protection of Young Persons Act (Germany)</a>
          </div> </td>
        </tr>

         <td align="center">16 <sup>(beer, wine and cider)</sup><br>18 <sup>(spirits)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-Gibraltar_164-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gibraltar-164">[164]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-Gibraltar_164-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gibraltar-164">[164]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited to sell alcohol drinks to anyone under the age of 18, other than the following two exceptions. The minimum age to be served in licensed premises is 16 if:<sup id="cite_ref-Gibraltar_164-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gibraltar-164">[164]</a></sup> 
          <ul>
           <li>The alcohol beverage is beer, wine or cider below 15% <a href="/wiki/ABV" class="mw-redirect" title="ABV">ABV</a>, <b>or</b></li> 
           <li>The alcohol beverage is served in a bottle, or a pre-packaged container below 5.5% <a href="/wiki/ABV" class="mw-redirect" title="ABV">ABV</a>.</li>
          </ul> </td>

Serving alcohol beverages to those under the age of 16 is a criminal offense and is punished with prison up to one year, if the individual is 16 or 17 it will be treated as an offense that is fined between €250 and €1000 <i>(Legge n. 189/2013)</i>. </td>

         <td>Alcohol possessed by minors may be confiscated as evidence. Drinking in public is prohibited, though this is rarely enforced in recreational areas.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">[179]</a></sup> </td>

         <td align="center">None<sup>(within designated drinking zones)</sup><br> Prohibited<sup>(elsewhere)</sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-tekst_jednolity:_Dz._U._2002_r._Nr_147_poz._1231_180-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tekst_jednolity:_Dz._U._2002_r._Nr_147_poz._1231-180">[180]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Article 15 of The Act on Upbringing in Sobriety and Counteracting Alcoholism<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">[181]</a></sup> prohibits sale or serving of alcohol beverages to anyone under 18 and that if doubt exists as to age, sellers/servers should require ID as proof of age. <p>Drinking in public places, with the exception of designated drinking zones, is prohibited regardless of age. </p> </td>

         <td colspan="2" align="center" style="background:Gainsboro">None </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-swe2010_190-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-swe2010-190">[190]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-sweden_191-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sweden-191">[191]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td align="center">20<sup id="cite_ref-swe2010_190-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-swe2010-190">[190]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Alcohol_in_Sweden" class="mw-redirect" title="Alcohol in Sweden">Alcohol in Sweden</a>
          </div>It is legal for anyone at any age to drink, but off-premise sale or supply to anyone under the age of 20 is prohibited and on-premise establishments are prohibited from serving alcohol beverages to anyone under 18. It is legal to serve an underage person alcohol in a private place, provided it's a limited amount and done in moderation.<sup id="cite_ref-swe2010_190-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-swe2010-190">[190]</a></sup> The reason for the lower limit in bars than in Systembolaget shops is that bartenders have a legal responsibility for how drunk a guest gets.<sup id="cite_ref-sweden_191-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sweden-191">[191]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

         <td colspan="2" rowspan="2" style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">16 <sup>(fermented beverages with up to 15% ABV and natural wines with up to 18% ABV)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">[192]</a></sup><br> 18 <sup>(spirits)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">[193]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Whoever offers or supplies alcohol beverages to a child under the age of 16 years in an amount which is harmful to one's health is punished with imprisonment up to 3 years or a fine.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">[194]</a></sup> Whoever sells or supplies spirits to a person under the age of 18 years is punished with a fine up to 10.000 CHF.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">[195]</a></sup> </td>

         <td align="center">None / 5<sup id="cite_ref-uk_198-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uk-198">[198]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-uk_198-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uk-198">[198]</a></sup> 16 <sup>(beer, wine or cider with meal and if accompanied by adult)</sup><sup id="cite_ref-scotland_199-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scotland-199">[199]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">18 <sup id="cite_ref-uk_198-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uk-198">[198]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td> 
          <ul>
           <li>It is prohibited to sell, serve, or offer alcohol beverages in licensed premises to anyone under the age of 18,<sup id="cite_ref-uk_198-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uk-198">[198]</a></sup> but minors aged 16–17 may consume wine, beer or cider on licensed premises when ordered with a meal and they are accompanied by an adult. Minors are prohibited to consume alcohol beverages in public.</li> 
           <li>Import: People over 17 are entitled to a duty-free allowance for alcohol beverages.</li>
          </ul> </td>
        </tr>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Flag_of_Scotland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Scotland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None </td> 
         <td align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-scotland_199-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scotland-199">[199]</a></sup> 16 <sup>(beer, wine or cider with meal if accompanied by adult))</sup><sup id="cite_ref-scotland_199-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scotland-199">[199]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" align="center">18<sup id="cite_ref-scotland_199-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scotland-199">[199]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td> 
          <ul>
           <li>It is prohibited to sell, serve, or offer alcohol beverages to anyone under the age of 18, but minors aged 16–17 may consume wine, beer or cider on licensed premises when ordered with a meal and they are accompanied by an adult. Minors are prohibited to consume alcohol beverages in public.<sup id="cite_ref-Licensing_Act_2005_200-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Licensing_Act_2005-200">[200]</a></sup></li> 
           <li>Import: People over 17 are entitled to a duty-free allowance for alcohol beverages.<sup id="cite_ref-UK_Duty_Free_201-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UK_Duty_Free-201">[201]</a></sup></li>
          </ul> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:Gainsboro" align="center">None </td> 
         <td colspan="3" align="center">18 </td> 
         <td>It is prohibited to sell, serve, or offer alcohol beverages to anyone under the age of 18. Minors are prohibited to consume alcohol beverages in public. </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="5"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> </td> 
         <td>Under the <a href="/wiki/British_Beer_and_Pub_Association" title="British Beer and Pub Association">BBPA</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Challenge_21" title="Challenge 21">Challenge 21 and Challenge 25</a> schemes, customers attempting to buy alcohol beverages are asked to prove their age if in the retailer's opinion they look under 21<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">[202]</a></sup> (or optionally 25) even though the law states they must be a minimum of 18. Many supermarket and off-licence chains display Challenge 21 (or Challenge 25) notices stating that they will not serve people who look under 21 (or 25) without ID. </td>
        </tr>

Minors buying, consuming or attempting to buy alcohol are committing an offence. The law provides an exception for the consumption of alcohol by minors as part of a religiously recognized ceremony.<sup id="cite_ref-Palau_Alcoholic_Beverage_Control_Act_214-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Palau_Alcoholic_Beverage_Control_Act-214">[214]</a></sup> </td>

         <td>It is prohibited for a minor to purchase, consume or attempt to purchase alcohol beverages. Any licence holder has to ensure that the customer who he sells or serves alcohol to, is at least 18 years of age.         </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Tonga.svg/23px-Flag_of_Tonga.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Tonga.svg/35px-Flag_of_Tonga.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Tonga.svg/46px-Flag_of_Tonga.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="960" data-file-height="480">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Tonga" title="Tonga">Tonga</a> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18<sup id="cite_ref-Tonga_Liquor_Licensing_Act_219-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tonga_Liquor_Licensing_Act-219">[219]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>Selling, serving or supplying alcohol to anyone under 18 years is prohibited. It is also prohibited for minors to buy, attempt to buy or consume alcohol in any public place and any violation of this law is punishable by a $1,000 fine.<sup id="cite_ref-Tonga_Liquor_Licensing_Act_219-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tonga_Liquor_Licensing_Act-219">[219]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="2"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Vanuatu.svg/23px-Flag_of_Vanuatu.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Vanuatu.svg/35px-Flag_of_Vanuatu.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Vanuatu.svg/46px-Flag_of_Vanuatu.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="360">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Vanuatu" title="Vanuatu">Vanuatu</a> </td> 
         <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">18<sup id="cite_ref-Vanuatu_Liquor_Licensing_Act_220-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vanuatu_Liquor_Licensing_Act-220">[220]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td>It is unlawful to sell, serve or supply alcohol to any person under the age of 18 years. Violation of the law is fined up to VT 25,000 or by a term of imprisonment not exceeding 3 months, or by both, fine and imprisonment. Any minor under the age of 18 years, being found in possession or consumption of alcohol is fined up to VT 10,000.<sup id="cite_ref-Vanuatu_Liquor_Licensing_Act_220-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vanuatu_Liquor_Licensing_Act-220">[220]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table>

        <li id="cite_note-IARD-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-IARD_1-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-IARD_1-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a
